  background-color: #d4edda;
  border-color: #c3e6cb;
}

.alert-danger {
  color: #721c24;
  background-color: #f8d7da;
  border-color: #f5c6cb;
}

.alert-warning {
  color: #856404;
  background-color: #fff3cd;
  border-color: #ffeeba;
}

.alert-info {
  color: #0c5460;
  background-color: #d1ecf1;
  border-color: #bee5eb;
}
```

  .container {
    max-width: 540px;
  }
}

@media (min-width: 768px) {
  .container {
    max-width: 720px;
  }
}

@media
```

            <label className="form-label">Password</label>
            <input 
              type="password" 
              className="form-control" 
              value={password} 
              onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
```
